## Pilot Notes

- Comment threads materially changed classification quality for `#6022`. Without comments, the issue looks like a generic Android keyboard complaint. With comments, it becomes a concrete selection-sync failure with operation evidence.
- `#6038` proves the ledger needs to tolerate maintainer-authored architecture issues, not just user bug reports.
- The schema is already good enough to separate:
  - user pain
  - likely root-cause layer
  - immediate maintainer action
  - v2 architectural relevance

## Current Schema Gaps

- `recurrence` stays weak in an open-only pilot. That field only becomes useful after the closed-issue pass.
- `test seam` may need a stricter enum family later if prose drift starts creeping back in.
- `likely-invalid` plus `ready-now` is legitimate but slightly counterintuitive; we may want a future distinction between current-contract invalidity and v2-target candidacy.
- `test seam` and `benchmark seam` may eventually want a shared implementation-seam vocabulary if the prose starts drifting.
